@hidden.valley PICKLE RANCH CUBAN SLIDERS! 😍
 
Ingredients:
-King’s Hawaiian Original Hawaiian Sweet Rolls
-Hidden Valley Pickle Flavored Ranch Dressing
-Hidden Valley Ranch Seasoning 
-2 tbsp Dijon mustard
-6 tbsp butter (melted)
-2 tsp minced garlic
-Ham
-Swiss cheese
- @grillospickles Dill Pickle Chips
 
Preparation:
1. Mix Dijon mustard, Hidden Valley Pickle Flavored Ranch Dressing, and about a third of the melted butter
2. Mix melted butter, minced garlic, and Hidden Valley Ranch Seasoning
3. Cut King’s Hawaiian Original Hawaiian Sweet Rolls in half (lengthwise), then spread mustard pickle ranch mixture on the inside of rolls
4. Assemble sliders with ham, Swiss cheese, and Grillo’s Dill Pickle Chips
5. Place top rolls on, then brush with ranch butter
6. Cover sliders with foil and bake at 350 for 15 minutes, then remove foil and bake an additional 5 minutes

sandwich of the summer - BLP (bacon lettuce pickle). She is absolutely divine not sure why I haven’t been crushing these for my entire life. 

-Toasted sourdough 
-@grillospickles pickle chips 
-Lettuce mixture: finely chopped lettuce, thinly sliced red onion, dill to taste, 1/2 tbsp pickle juice, 1 tbsp mayo, salt, pepper, red pepper flakes
-bacon (however many slices you want on 1 sandy). I do my bacon in the oven because it’s superior. Heat to 375 and bake on a sheet pan with tinfoil for 15-20 minutes flipping halfway through. Enjoy pickle fam!

DILL PICKLE CREAM CHEESE WONTONS - quick lil appetizer or whole damn meal if you’re feelin frisky 😈 

-Wonton wrappers (however many you want to make) 

MIXINS: 
cream cheese 
fresh dill 
chopped @grillospickles pickle chips 
chives 
garlic powder
salt 

FOR THE SAUCE:
1/4 cup chili onion crunch 
2 tbsp hot honey 
1 tbsp pickle juice 

Spoon 1 tbsp into each won ton wrapper, rub the edges with water or pickle juice, seal it up. Spray with olive oil or avocado oil and air fry at 390 for 6-8 minutes (check half way for doneness)

Make your sauce while frying. Whisk together chili onion crunch, hot honey, and pickle juice 

If you want to deep fry these, get a pot and fill with vegetable oil and heat to 375 degrees, drop in your wontons until golden brown.

Dill pickle chicken salad 💪

Follow @lainiecooks for more easy high protein recipes! 

This is the best and easiest chicken salad I’ve ever made, and if your pickle lover like me, you will be absolutely obsessed. 

What you’ll need:
2 1/2 cups of chopped rotisserie chicken 
1/2 cup @grillospickles pickle de galllo 
1 tbsp olive oil 
1/2 cup full fat Greek yogurt 
1 tsp dried dill 
1/2 tsp garlic powder 
1/2 tsp salt 
1/4 tsp pepper 
Lettuce cups 
Garnish with @getgraza new potato chips and finishing olive oil 

Instructions: 
To a large bowl, add rotisserie chicken. Add all other ingredients and mix well. Serve on lettuce cups and top with crushed potato chips and a drizzle of olive oil. Great for meal prep and makes about 4-5 servings.

#healthylunchideas #mealprep #mealprepideas #chickensalad #mealprepping #pickles #picklelover #lettucecups

#ad Bringing Grillo’s Pickles and Cheez-It together again for the Cheez-It Fried Pickle Dip of your DREAMS to get you ready for this weekend.🥒🧀🏀

1 cup crushed Extra Toasty Cheez-It crackers
3 tablespoons unsalted butter
4 tablespoons fresh dill, divided Kosher salt, to taste
Freshly ground black pepper, to taste 8 ounces cream cheese, softened
1 cup sour cream
1 cup Grillo’s Pickle de Gallo, plus 2 tablespoons brine
1 tablespoon fresh chives, thinly sliced
2 teaspoons garlic powder
1 teaspoon onion powder
Extra Big Cheez-It crackers, for serving

➡️Place Cheez-It crackers in a zip top bag and use a rolling pin to coarsely crush.

➡️Melt butter in a skillet over medium heat. Add Cheez-It crumbs and toast until golden brown.
Transfer crumbs to a medium bowl and mix with 2 tablespoons fresh dill. Season with salt and pepper.

➡️In a medium bowl, combine cream cheese and sour cream. Mix together until fully combined and smooth. Add pickle de gallo, pickle juice, dill, chives, garlic powder, and onion powder. Stir together.
Season with salt and pepper.

➡️Pour mixture into a serving bowl and smooth top.
Pour toasted Cheez-It crumbs over the dip in an even layer and serve with Extra Big Cheez-It crackers. 

#cheezit #pickledip #grillos #asmr #recipe #appetizers #snacks #gamedayfood

🤩 @grillospickles PICKLE DIP!
(with toasted roll crisps)! 🍞
 
Ingredients:
-King’s Hawaiian Original Hawaiian Sweet Rolls
-Olive oil
-1 c chopped @grillospickles Dill Pickle Chips
-8 oz cream cheese, softened
-1 c sour cream
-1/4 c pickle juice
-1 tbsp ranch seasoning
-1/4 c pickle juice
-1 tbsp fresh chives
-1 tbsp fresh dill
-1/4 tsp salt
-1/2 c crushed @bouldercanyon Boulder Batch Avocado Oil Grillo’s Classic Dill Pickle Kettle Potato Chips
 
Preparation:
1. Slice King’s Hawaiian Original Hawaiian Sweet Rolls individually into 4-5 slices (each), then drizzle with olive oil and bake at 350 for about 8-10 minutes (flip halfway)
2. Combine softened cream cheese, sour cream, and pickle juice, then add minced garlic, ranch seasoning, fresh chives, fresh dill, and salt
3. Once well combined, mix in chopped @grillospickles Dill Pickle Chips, and crushed Boulder Batch Avocado Oil Grillo’s Classic Dill Pickle Kettle Potato Chips
4. Finish dip with additional crushed kettle potato chips and fresh dill on top, then serve with toasted roll crisps

DILL PICKLE CHICKEN AND WAFFLES WITH CHIPOTLE MAPLE RANCH - your new favorite appetizer. I used Grillo’s pickles for the THREE different pickle components for this recipe. Let’s get into it.

What you’ll need:
-Chicken breast
-@grillospickles dill pickle slices 
-Frozen mini waffles 
-Dill pickle potato chips (I used the @grillospickles and @bouldercanyon dill pickle potato chip collab)
-1 cup Greek yogurt
-2 tbsp buttermilk 
-1.5 tbsp Ranch seasoning (I just used the packet)
-2 tbsp Chipotle pepper sauce 
-1 tbsp Maple syrup 
-2 tbsp water 
-salt
-pepper
-2 eggs
-1 cup flour 
-toothpicks

Cut your chicken breasts into small bite sized pieces (cut as many as you want to serve. I used 2 chicken breast and got about 16 pieces). Put chicken breast into a bowl and pour over pickle juice until chicken is covered. Cover and place in the fridge for 2 hours). 

Make your chipotle maple ranch - in a small bowl mix your greek yogurt, buttermilk, ranch seasoning, sauce from your chipotle pepper can, maple syrup, water, and a pinch of salt. Blend or mix well. Set in the fridge. 

blend or food process your potato chips to get them crushed up like a breading. Get your dredging station ready - scrambled eggs in one bowl, and flour in another. strain and dry your chicken pieces. Drop one at a time in flour and cover well, drop into egg mixture, and then cover in chip crumbs, set on a plate to the side. Do this with all of your chicken chunks. 

In a skillet over medium heat, heat avocado oil (or vegetable oil - something with a high smoke point). Once oil is hot, add in your chicken pieces and cook on one side until golden brown. Flip the pieces and brown the other side. Get the sides too! Make sure these are browned and crispy. Remove from oil and set on a cooling rack. 

Heat your mini waffles according the instructions on the packaging. Put a pickle on eat waffle, top with a piece of chicken, and stick with a toothpick. Dip into your chipotle maple ranch. Enjoy!

Claymation made by the one and only @boredmonkeyshow
Calling all dill pickle lovers!! These were INCREDIBLE. Who knew we needed this collab so bad?🥒 @chosenfoods @grillospickles

Ingredients: 
• Chosen Foods 100% Pure Avocado Oil for frying 
• Grillo’s Pickles, sliced into 1 inch pieces 
•  1 cup all purpose flour 
• ½ teaspoon salt 
• 1 teaspoon ground black pepper 
• ¼ teaspoon paprika 
• ¼ teaspoon cayenne pepper 
• ¼ teaspoon garlic powder 
• ½ cup buttermilk 
• 1 large egg 

Sauce: 
• 2 Tablespoons Chosen Foods Classic Mayo 
• 1 Tablespoon BBQ sauce 
• 1 teaspoon ketchup 
• 1 teaspoon hot sauce 
• ½ teaspoon ground black pepper 
• Fill a Dutch oven or heavy-bottomed saucepan 2-3” deep with oil for frying. Oil will need to reach 375F 
• Meanwhile, prepare your breading mixture by whisking together flour, salt, pepper, paprika, cayenne pepper, and garlic powder.
• In a separate bowl, whisk together buttermilk and egg 
• Coat slices in flour mixture, gently shake off excess, dredge in buttermilk/egg mixture, then coat with flour mixture again. 
• Transfer (carefully!) to oil and fry pickle slices until golden brown. 
• Use a slotted spoon or strainer to remove from oil and transfer to a paper towel lined plate. 
• Best enjoyed warm. Serve with dipping sauce! 

#chosenfoods #avocado #avocadooil #holiday #holidayshopping #pickles #dillpickle #grillospickles #friedpickles #appetizer #easyrecipe #foodporn #fried

I tested the viral recipe for the CHICKLE 🙌 and now it’s your turn…

4 pickle spears
2 cups shredded cheddar
1/2 cup dipping sauce like a ranch

See recipe - https://sipbitego.com/viral-chickle

After some practice, here’s what I suggest: 

The key is to make a really thin shredded cheese layer (use med-high heat) and work quickly to wrap the pickle inside. 

Use two spatulas to gently mold the cheese to stick to itself. 

Don’t forget the dip! Try the Sip Bite Go recipe for jalapeno ranch - it’s a perfect match.

Learn how to make better food at home… follow @sipbitego…

🍕PICKLE PIZZA SNACK HACK ⬇️
MINI PICKLE PIZZA TOASTS! 🍕

Ingredients:
-King’s Hawaiian Original Hawaiian Sweet Rolls
- @grillospickles Classic Dill Pickle Chips
-Olive oil
-Alfredo sauce
-Mozzarella cheese
-Dill (fresh or dried)
-Crushed red pepper
-Ranch dressing

Preparation:
1. Slice King’s Hawaiian Original Hawaiian Sweet Rolls individually into 4-5 slices (each), then drizzle with olive oil and bake at 350 for about 8-10 minutes (flip halfway)
2. Add alfredo sauce, mozzarella cheese, @grillospickles Classic Dill Pickle Chips to toasted roll slices, then bake at 350 for 7-8 minutes
3. Top with dill and crushed red pepper, then enjoy with ranch dressing

PICKLEBALL 🥒 

Dill with it. Pickles make everything better. 

The gin brings botanical and juniper notes, while the dry vermouth adds a subtle herbal complexity. @grillospickles contributes a tangy and savory layer, enhancing the overall crisp and refreshing taste.

PICKLEBALL 🥒 
1.5oz dry gin 
1oz dry vermouth (@drinksbyevie x @drinkveso )
.75oz pickle brine 
.5oz sūpāsawā (@supasawaco )
soda water 

Combine all ingredients into glass with ice. Top with soda water and stir gently and briefly to combine

We teamed up to create the ultimate new year snack: high-protein, low carb, and delicious! Check out the recipe for these Tuna Pickle Sliders below.

Tuna Salad Recipe:

1 can Wild Planet Albacore tuna

¼ cup Mayonnaise

2 Tbsp Dijon Mustard

Juice of ¼ lemon

1 small rib of celery, diced

¼ small red onion, diced

Handful of fresh dill, chopped

2 tsp capers

Salt & black pepper

Mix all of the above ingredients together to make a salad.

To make the sliders:

Place a small piece of lettuce on a Grillo’s pickle chip

Top with tuna salad and a chunk of white cheddar cheese

Optional to top with another pickle chip, and then spear with a toothpick to hold it all together

Introducing our “Pickle Maria”, Bloody Mary’s cheeky sister 😮‍💨 She’s briny and smooth with a little kick, and is sure to catch some eyes (and tastebuds) 😜 Make it for brunch or lunch, or any time you want! All we know is that you’ll enjoy ✨🫒🤝 Recipe below:
Pickle Maria
4 oz Green Mix
1½ oz Tequila Blanco
¾ oz @Grillospickles Brine (classic)
¼ oz Worcestershire Sauce
2 dashes of Green Hot Sauce 
Pinch of Celery Salt
Pinch of Black Pepper
Garnish:
Salt & Pepper rim, Grillos Pickle Spear, Skewer of Olives, Dill Sprig 🥒🫒🌿
Green Mix (4 servings)
Ingredients:
• 4 tomatillos, peeled and rinsed
• 1/2 medium white onion, quartered
• 1 jalapeño, stem removed
• 3 cloves of garlic, skin on
• 3-4 tablespoons of @getgraza ‘Sizzle’ olive oil
• 1 teaspoon sea salt
Instructions:
1. Preheat oven to the high broil setting.
2. Prepare the Vegetables:
• Peel and rinse the tomatillos.
• Peel and quarter the onion.
• Remove the stem from the jalapeño.
3. Arrange the prepared vegetables on a baking sheet and drizzle them evenly with the Graza ‘Sizzle’ olive oil.
4. Place the baking sheet in the preheated oven and broil for approximately 10-15 minutes. Watch for the vegetables to develop some color and slightly char.
5. Remove the sheet from the oven and let the roasted vegetables cool for a few minutes. Once they are cool enough to handle, peel the skin from the garlic cloves. 
6. Place all the roasted vegetables in a blender with salt and blend until fully pureed.
7. Once chilled, your Pickle Maria mix is ready!

Pickle Travel Hack 🥒
Cuz we can’t live without @grillospickles 

Did you know that you can bring a food bag IN ADDITION to your carry on and personal bag?
I learned this trick last year and let me tell you, it’s a game changer!

Howeverrrr you want to make sure that you are only carrying FOOD and NOT liquid. So instead of wasting that precious pickle brine I’m turning it into some pickled shishito pepperz for when I get back. 🔥

I did bring some other lil snackies, but idk @grillospickles Classic Dill Pickle Spears are pretty perfect all on their own. 🤤

If you can’t eat your perishables right away just bring an extra ziplock bag and fill it with ice once you’re through security. 

*make sure to check your airports guidelines before traveling 😘

#travel #traveltips #pickles #snacking #airport #vacaction #happy

Smoked Tri-Tip Sandwich and a Cold IPA 

I don’t know of a better combo than BBQ and craft beer. This is my attempt to recreate my go-to sando from my favorite craft BBQ spot here in Orange County: @heritagebarbecue .

BBQ Sando and beer:

Smoked Tri-Tip on a toasted brioche bun, Grillos Dill Pickles, homemade slaw, and paired with my homemade Grapefruit Cold IPA 🫡.

SLAW RECIPE:

+ Red and Green cabbage, ½ head of each, shredded
+ Carrot, 2 shredded
+ Mayo, ½ cup
+ Half and Half, ½ cup
+ Fresh lemon juice, 2 TBSP
+ Maple syrup, raw & dark, 2 TBSP
+ Sea salt, ½ TSP

Creamy ranch pickle dip! This is soooo simple and delicious, PLUS Grillo’s Pickles are a great 0 point snack on @ww !! Highly recommend trying it with the spicy pickles to add a lil extra kick 🔥

Recipe:

2 tbsp fresh parsley, finely chopped 
2 Tbsp scallions or chives, finely chopped
1 tsp dill, chopped
½ tsp black pepper 
¼ tsp salt
1 clove(s) garlic, grated

Mini Chicken n’ Wafflez Sliderz wit BLAZING Hot @grillospickles 🔥🥒

Stop whatever you’re doing and make these…. SERIOUSLY 🥵

The BLAZING Hot Pickle chips on top just rocket ship these sliderz to the moon. 
And have you ever seen a hawaiian roll turned waffle?! It’s genius. 

So yeah… go make ‘em. 😘

1 large chicken breast, about 1/2 lb
1 cup flour
1 tsp salt
1 tsp smoked paprika
1/2 tsp garlic powder
1/4 tsp onion powder
1/4 tsp turmeric
1/4 mustard powder
Fresh cracked black pep
1/4 cup milk 
1 egg
Vegetable Oil
Hawaiian Rolls
Maple Syrup
BLAZING Hot @grillospickles

Fill up a heavy bottomed pot with vegetable oil and set over medium heat. We want it to reach a temp around 350F.

Pound the chicken breast to about 1/4 in thickness and cut it into 6 pieces. 

Mixie mix all of the dry ingredients (flour and spices) in one bowl and wet ingredients (milk and egg) in another bowl. 
Spoon about 2 tbsp of the milk mixture into the dry and give that a lil mix. This will help you get those crispy crunchy bitz on the chicken. 

Dredge the chicken in the flour mixture, shake off excess, then in the milky mixture, shake off excess, then back in the dry, really pressing it into the flour to fully adhere. Repeat with all chicken pieces. TIP: keep one hand wet and one dry so you don’t turn into a sticky mushy mess. 👼🏻
Let those hang out for a bit while you waffle-ize your rollz.

Smoosh one roll in the waffle maker at a time and cook on the lowest heat setting (or whatever setting gives ya a crispy, golden, but not burnt “waffle”) 
Repeat until you have 6 waffles. 

Okie dokie… let’s fry dat chicken. Timing will vary depending on the exact temp of your oil, but expect to deep fry these for about 3-5 minutes. You want CRISPY, golden, and a minimum internal temp of 160F. Drain on a wire rack and immediately sprinkle with extra salt. 

Assemblyyyyyy! Literally just waffle, chicken, pickle chips, and a gennnnerous drizzle of maple syrup. 

ENJOY!

#ad #pickles #appetizer #fried #cooking #happy

Pickle De Gallo LOBSTER Roll Sliderz🦞🥒

Y’all… @grillospickles Pickle De Gallo Lobster Rollz just hit different. 
And they’re soooo adorable in slider form. I could straight up eat all four in one sitting. 🤤

Get the Pickle De Gallo at Wegmans, Harris Teeter, and Target. 🔥

3 lobster tails, cooked (approx 10oz total in shell)
1 tbsp celery, finely diced to be about the same size as the pickle de gallo
2 tbsp chives, sliced into super teeny tiny chivey tubez, divided
4 tbsp pickle de Gallo, divided
1 tbsp pickle de Gallo juice
1-2 tbsp mayo
Salt and pep to season
4 hawaiian rolls @kingshawaiian

Steam yo lobstaz!! I did mine in a steamer basket for 6 minutes. 
However you decide to cook them, you just need the meat!

You can absotootly just shred all of the lobster, but I like the different textures so I chopped one tail and shredded (wit muh handz) the other two. 
You want the pieces pretty small cause… sliderz. 

Combine the celery, 1 tbsp chives, 2 tbsp pickle de gallo, pickle de gallo juiceee, 1 tbsp mayo, and lobster in a bowl. 
*start with 1 tbsp mayo and add more if you want it* 
Season with salt and pep. Mixie mix. 

Toast your rolls in some butter over medium heat, about 1 minute. 

Then assemble! Divide the lobster mix in 4 and evenly distribute among the 4 sliders. Add about 1/2 tbsp pickle de gallo on top of each one, then evenly divide and top with the remaining 1 tbsp chives. Put the bun tops back on and boom! Slider. 😎

10k likes and maybe we’ll make this pickle pizza for real 😎 Bonus: we’ll send one lucky liker some @eatbanza and @grillospickles goodies to recreate this at home. Recipe: 

Banza x Grillo’s Pickle Pizza

Ingredients:
1/4 cup Alfredo sauce
2-3 tablespoons Grillo’s Pickle de Gallo
1-2 cloves garlic, chopped
1 Banza Pizza Crust
1/4 cup shredded sharp white cheddar
10-12 Grillo’s Pickle Chips
1 tbsp. chopped dill
(Optional) additional Pickle de Gallo and fresh dill, for garnish

1. Prepare sauce: Preheat oven to 400F. Combine Alfredo sauce, Pickle de Gallo, and garlic in a small bowl.
2. Top pizza: Spread sauce on top of pizza crust. Top with cheese, pickles, and dill. Bake for 12-15 minutes, or until crust is golden brown and cheese is melted and bubbly.
3. (Optional) Top with more Pickle de Gallo and fresh dill, if using. Slice and enjoy!

Tips: Use a mix of spicy and non-spicy pickles for a surprise in every bite :)

BLAZING HOT Pickle Tuna Bitez 🔥

These BLAZING HOT Pickle Tuna Bitez are the perfect lil snacky snack for this holiday weekend (or literally any time, day, place, planet) 🪐

Plus the @grillospickles BLAZING Hot Pickle Chips are 🔥🔥🔥 and popping up at Stop and Shop, Harris Teeter, Wakefern, and Nugget Markets. 

Here’s how ya do it 💃
PS - It’ll make approximately 16-20 bitez

FILLING:
2 4oz Cans o’ tuna
6 blazing hot pickle chips, super duper finely chopped
1/4 cup mayo
1 tsp pickle juice, try to get some dill n stuff in it
1 tsp olive oil, or just drizzle till your heart is content
Salt n pep to taste

Mixie mix everything, trying to get the tuna as crushed up as possible (hands work great here). 

LIL BITEZ:
Buttery crackers, or any crackers that makes you happy
MOREEE pickle chips
And your tuna mix doiiii

Ok so assembly goes cracker, some tuna, pickle, more tuna, cracker. 
Dats it. 

ENJOY 🕺🏻

Grillo’s Grilled CHEEESE 😮‍💨

If you’re not putting @Grillospickles SANDWICH MAKERS on your Grilled chzzzz what are you even doing?

Here’s how I did it 😎

Get you some bread (I used @angelicbakehouse), some chzzzz (I used @cabot CHEDDAR and @andrewandeverett MOZZZ), butter for the pan, and OBVS pickle sammi makers. 
I used two pickle slices per sammi, but add as many as your little heart desires. We won’t judge. 🤤

You want this to toast low and slow so the chzzz has ample time to melt without the bread burning. We’re talking medium-low heat y’all. Pop a lid on it to encourage the chz to melt even more. 

If you want to achieve that melty, chzzz pull affect I highly recommend adding mozz in the mix. 
Allsooooo after you slice it you may break the “cheese pull” so if you want that, pop it back in the pan for a minute on each side so the cheese can melt back together. Idk, pro tip?

That’s really all there is to it.

GO MAKE ONE.

Sweet n Spicy PICKLE Spam Sliderz 😮‍💨

AVAILABLE at Target and will also be at the NYC pop up shop June 3rd - 18th 🔥🥒

You’re a real one if you remember that these Sweet n Spicy pickle chips were the @Grillospickles new flavor!!
@Grillospickles went so hard with em. 🔥

Ok the sliderz. We’re making a special sauce with finely diced pickle chips instead of sweet relish… which is PHENOM. Spam is a no brainer. A hefty stack of the Sweet n Spicy pickle chips is a must. Hawaiian rolls just tie it all together. 

Da Special Sauce:
2 tbsp finely diced pickle chips (about 5-6 chips PLUS a lil pepper bit if you’re feeling fun)
1 tbsp lemon juice
2 cloves garlic, garlic pressed, minced, or grated
1/2 cup mayo
1/4 cup ketchup
1ish tbsp worcestershire (yes, I googled how to spell that)
1ish tbsp dijon mustard

Mixie mix and you’re good to go. 😘

Da Sliderz: (8 sammies)
1 can of Spam - cut in half length wise, then in 4’s width wise (8 pieces)
Sweet n Spicy Pickle chips: 2-3 per slider
8 hawaiian rolls

I cooked the spam over medium high heat in a cast iron skillet with some oil in it. Cook about 3 minutes on each side, or until browning and crisping. 
I also toasted the buns in the same pan, cause mmmm spam fat. Keep a close eye on the rolls because they brown/burn QUICKLY. 
Then assemble! Bun, spam, sauce, pickles, bun. Done 😎

oh and can we just appreciate the fact that my pickle juice stains fully disappeared. love it.

Deviled Eggs w/ Grillo’s Pickle de Gallo 😮‍💨

Pickle de Gallo takes these eggz to a whole other level y’all. 
The brine adds some tang to the filling while the actual mixie mix on top provides a flavor and textural explosion.

These eggiez are addicting and so so so easy to make. 
Double it, triple it, quadruple it… they’re that good. 🤤

INGREDIENTS:
6 hard boiled eggs
1 tsp mustard - I used yellow here, but dijon would slap too
2 tbsp mayo - I used avocado mayo here, but you do you
1 1/2 tsp Pickle de Gallo brine/juice
Pickle de Gallo for topping the eggz
Salt n pep for seasoning

Boil dem eggz. Bring water to boil, add eggz making sure they have water coving them. Turn heat off and let sit for 11 minutes. 
Remove the eggs and immediately place them in an ice bath to cool. This will make peeling the eggs a lot easier. 
Once cooled, peel, cut in half, remove the yolks adding them to a bowl, and rinse the whites to remove excess yolk. 

To the egg yolk bowl add: mustard, mayo, Pickle de Gallo juice, and salt and pep to season. Mash that up with a spoon or fork until it is nice and smooth with hardly any bumps remaining. 
You can either dollop the yolk mix back into the egg whites orrrrr spoon it into a ziplock bag, cut off the tip, and pipe it into the whites. 
Top with a little bit (or a lot and just really go for it) of Pickle de Gallo and boom, you’re done!

#pickles #eggs #appetizer #snacks #grillos #grillospickles
If you don’t drink the brine out the jar with a straw, you’re not reaching your full pickle potential. Bravo @kellyspilates you win 🏆 

#fresh #pickles #grillos #pickle #grillospickles #worldsbest #picklejuice #brine #drink #pickleball

Ham N Chz Grillo’s THICKLE Pickles! 😮‍💨

Ham, Mozzarella Cheese, and @Grillospickles THICKLE Pickles!! 🤤

And guess what?! THICKLES are now available at all Aldi locations!! 
Available in both the OG Dill and HOT 🥵 
@aldiusa

These are stupid easy and the bestest lil snack. Perf with OG Dill or HOT. 🔥

Easiest to roll up with thinly sliced ham, but you do you. 
Take one piece of ham, put a lil shredded mozzarella in the center, add a THICKLE, top it with a little more mozz, then fold that baby up. 
Add a little bit of oil to a pan set over medium heat and cook seam side down first until nice and crispy, about 2-4 minutes. Flip and repeat. 
Dats it! You should be left with a crispy, melty, cheesy pickle party. 

ENJOY that pickle pocket of greatness. 😎

This snack is going to be a slam dunk for this weekend.. 👀🏀🔥

Cheez-It Crusted Oven Fried @grillospickles 
 
For the pickles:
3 cups of Cheez-It Crackers 
1 tablespoon dried dill
2 teaspoon garlic powder
1 teaspoon kosher salt
1 (16-ounce) container Grillo’s Class Dill Pickle Chips
2 large egg whites
3 tablespoons olive oil
Ranch or creamy dill dip for serving
 
Arrange a rack in the middle of the oven and heat to 450°F. Place a rimmed baking sheet on the rack to preheat while you prepare the pickles.
 
Add Cheez-it Crackers to a zip-top bag with dill, garlic powder, and salt, and seal tightly. Use a heavy skillet or rolling pin to crush the Cheez-It Crackers to a fine crumb.
 
Drain the pickles well and pat them dry with paper towels to remove as much moisture as possible (save the pickle juice for marinades, cocktails, sauces, and dressings!).
 
Place the egg whites in a medium bowl and whisk until foamy and white, about 5 minutes. Add the pickles to the egg whites and gently stir with a spatula to coat. Use a slotted spoon to transfer the pickles to the bag. Seal again and shake the bag to coat the pickles evenly in the Cheez-It mixture.
 
Drizzle the olive oil on the preheated baking sheet. Working quickly, remove the pickles from the bag, shaking off any excess Cheez-It mixture, and place on the baking sheet, making sure they are spaced evenly and not touching. Bake until golden brown and crisp, 20-25 minutes, rotating and flipping the pickles as needed every 10 minutes.
 
Transfer the pickles to a serving platter and serve warm with ranch or creamy dill dip.

This Smoked Tri-Tip Sandwich by @ryanmichaelcarter is nothing fancy, just a bunch of calories in beautiful sandwich form.
+ Smoked tri-tip
+ Colby Jack cheese + @grillospickles dill pickles
+ Asiago cheese ciabatta roll
The tri-tip was smoked on my @webergrills Smokey Mountain at 225F over oak until it reached an internal 115F. Then seared on a cast-iron skillet for about 2 minutes on each side until internal temp reached 130F.

SillyJake Cooks: Fried Onion Cheeseburger Sliders with @grillospickles and @bolthousefarms 🍔🍔🍔
•
Truly some of the best pickles out there. So fresh, so crunchy. The perfect brightness for a cheesy fried onion burger. This ranch also low key blew me away. Made with yogurt and only 50 calories per serving but so rich, so creamy and so fricken good!!! You gotta try these sliders for game day this weekend. I devoured all 4 😅
I love you and @mslaurynhill loves you too ❤️
•
Slider Sauce
- Equal parts Bolthouse Farms Ranch and Grillo’s Pickle De Gallo. 

Ranch Fried Onions
Wet Batter: 
- 3/4 cup of Bolthouse Farms ranch 
- 1/2 cup of water 

Dry Batter: 
- 1 cup of AP flour 
- 2 tbsp garlic powder 
- 1 tbsp paprika 
- 1 tbsp salt 
- 1 tbsp black pepper 

Deep fry at 375 until golden brown and crispy.

Gochujang chicken sliders FTW 🤤

Slightly savory, spicy, and sweet with a fresh crunch of the worlds best pickle in every bite.

Try for yourself 🫡

Ingredients:
- @kingshawaiian Sweet Slider Buns
- @grillospickles Classic Dill Pickle Chips
-Chicken thighs (boneless/skinless)
-Salt
-Pepper
-Garlic
-1/4 cup soy sauce
-1 tablespoon Gochujang
-1 teaspoon sesame oil
-1 tablespoon honey
-1/4 cup honey
-1/4 cup brown sugar
-Sesame seeds

Preparation:
1. Season chicken thighs with salt, pepper, and
garlic powder and cook through until they
reach an internal temp of 165 degrees
2. To make Gochujang sauce, combine soy
sauce, Gochujang, sesame oil, honey, and
brown sugar
3. Pull apart chicken thighs and toss chicken
with the sauce, then finish with toasted sesame
seeds
4. Assemble sliders by adding a Grillo's Pickles
Classic Dill Pickle Chip to the bottom bun,
followed by the Gochujang chicken, and a drizzle of honey 🍯 

#grillospickles #grillos #pickles #pickle #fresh #gochujang
Hot dogs three ways on @kingshawaiian Original
Hawaiian Sweet Rolls topped with some fresh Grillo’s.. you can’t go wrong! Try for yourselves 

Here’s how to make them 

Chicago Style:
1. Cook hot dog on the grill
2. Take two Kings Hawaiian Original Hawalian Sweet
Rolls and cut down the top to make a slit
3. Add toppings to hot dog: 2 tomato wedges, 1
Grillo's Pickles Dill Pickle Spear, relish, diced onions,
2 sport peppers, ketchup

Chili Dog:
1. Cook hot dog on the grill
2. Take two Kings Hawaiian Original Hawaiian Sweet
Rolls and cut down the top to make a slit
3. Add toppings to hot dog: prepared chili (no
beans), Grillo's Pickles Pickle de Gallo, shredded
cheese

BBQ Dog:
1. Wrap bacon around hot dog and grill or smoke
until the bacon on the outside is crispy
2. Take two Kings Hawaiian Original Hawaiian Sweet
Rolls and cut down the top to make a slit
3. Place 2 Grillo's Pickles Classic Dill Pickle Chips on
bun, then add bacon-wrapped hot dog and a drizzle
of BBQ sauce

What happens when you up-cycle a cucumber? You get a pickle. And when you up-cycle vintage chocolate chip cookie desert camo suits and over dye then green you get “Pickle”camo.
 
We teamed up with artist, designer and friend Najeeb Sheikh @dasheikee to bring you this extremely limited edition of over-dyed "pickle" camouflage kits as well as some stonewashed vintage hoodies to balance out the collection. This collaboration highlights how much fun you can have with up-cycling your veggies into pickled greatness or old clothes into something fresh. Each garment is unique, just like every batch of our pickles.  Like our recipe, we took classic ingredients, added some Grillo's love and created something special to share with the world. All items sourced, dyed and assembled in Los Angeles, California

About the artist:
Matthew Langille is a New Jersey based artist known for his unique, whimsy and light hearted approach to illustration, pattern design and art. For the past seventeen years, Matthew has been working on global artist collaborations with some of the world's most exciting and well known brands. Today we are happy to announce the Matthew Langille x Grillo's capsule. This collection highlights Matthews' love for pickles in his own fun, unique perspective bringing to life the wonderful world of Grillo's Pickles.

A few weeks ago we got an email from @thehardwayhome who are ROWING A BOAT from MA ➡️ IRELAND… yes, you read that right! They wanted to bring pickles on their journey.. kind of like a “if you could bring 1 food with you to a desert island what would you bring” moment.. they tried making their own pickles but when they found Grillo’s they decided the attempt to make a better pickle was even more insane than the mission ahead of them.. @thehardwayhome wanted to bring pickles so it was only right we hooked them up and decided to be a sponsor on their wild adventure. People thought we were crazy for starting out of a pickle cart selling 2 spears for $1 and I’m sure people think @thehardwayhome are crazy for rowing a boat across the Atlantic but real recognize real and we are wishing them safe travels on this epic quest!! Shoot them a follow to see where they’re at over the next 2 months

Over the last decade it’s been a privilege to have Philadelphia’s finest @tripleplaysports1971 hand stitch all of our custom jerseys and gear!! 11 years ago I had the white jersey made. It’s been through the good, the bad, and the ugly.. I wore it on the streets and I’ve worn it to some of the biggest meetings of my life. This jersey keeps me grounded and true to myself. It’s a symbol of hard-work and passion. Never forget those who have been with you since day 1! Without them there would be no us and there would be no you to enjoy our product. This summer marks the 11th year anniversary of Grillo’s Pickles. It all started selling 2 spears for $1 of out of a hand built wooden pickle cart at the Park St T stop in the Boston Common. Thank you for all the love and support over the years and remember, always believe in yourself and go after what you love!💚

🚨PICKLE TRUFFLE OIL PIZZA🚨

a pre- made pizza crust, a Boboli, but you could always make your own and cook a bit before adding toppings.

1 16 inch prepared pizza crust

2 tablespoons ricotta 
1-2 tablespoons Olive Oil 
1 large clove crushed garlic

1 and 1/2 C mozzarella 
4-5 thinly sliced Grillos Hot Italian Spears, or any of your favorite Grillos sliced or diced

3-4 slices Hot Ham Capicola, chopped

White Truffle Oil (infused with Garlic if possible!) Optional:
Sprinkle of Parmesan
Salt and Pepper to taste 
Fresh Dill Weed 
Pre -heat oven to 425, Spread prepared crust with ricotta, olive oil and garlic, plus 3/4 cup mozzarella. Bake crust about 8 minutes, remove and top with pickles, capicola, remaining mozzarella, return to oven 2-3 minutes until lightly browned and bubbly around edges. Drizzle a tiny amount of White Truffle Oil over pizza- Less is More-go easy, keep a thumb over opening to control flow.
Sprinkle with dill weed and Parmesan if desired. Devour!

What word comes to your mind when you eat @grillospickles ? Shout out to our friends over at @delish 💚💚💚
The Hot Italian Dill is a very special flavored pickle made with fresh jalepeno and habanero peppers. We add garlic, dill, grape leaf, salt and water to remain true to our classic @grillospickles taste. 
The heat can best be described as “scenic heat” because you taste the flavor of the pickle then the heat emerges from the background,  much like the sun peaking over the horizon. Its a wonderful blend of flavors for any pallet young or old. 🌶🥒🔥 .
.
.
.
.

When CEO Travis Grillo looks back, he attributes his success to the humble advice he received from family, friends, and even strangers. The Grillo’s Pickles 2 Cents Project was created to give back to the communities that supported Travis as he grew his brand – starting in our very own hometown. This May through August, Grillo’s Pickles will donate two cents of every jar we sell in New England retailers to Boys & Girls Clubs of Boston. Help us meet our goal of $5,000! Then check back here next Tuesday to see how you could win prizes all summer long!

Add Grillo's to improve your culinary skills; Your friends are gonna think u really know what you're doing! 😜 
Toss 4 beets in a baking dish with olive oil, salt and pepper. Cover and roast at 425 degrees F until tender, about 40 minutes; let cool, then rub off the skins. Cut into wedges; toss with any juices from the baking dish, capers, chopped Grillo's, a dash each of Worcestershire and hot sauce, and chopped parsley.
